 If the Defending Pokémon has any Energy cards attached to it, flip 1 coin. If heads, choose 1 of those Energy cards and discard it.
 Search your deck for 1 Basic Pokémon card named this Pokemon or Nidoran ♂ and put it onto your Bench. Shuffle your deck afterward. You cant use this attack if your Bench is full.
 Discard all Lightning Energy cards attached to this Pokemon. This attack does 20 damage plus 10 more damage for each Energy card discarded in this way.
 Flip 3 coins. If you get 1 heads, this attack does 10 damage plus 10 more damage. If you get 2 heads, this attack does 10 damage plus 30 more damage. If you get 3 heads, this attack does 10 damage plus 60 more damage.
 Search your deck for 1 Baby Pokémon or Basic Pokémon card and put it onto your Bench. Shuffle your deck afterward. You cant use this attack if your Bench is full.
 If your opponent has any Benched Pokémon, choose up to 2 of them. This attack does 10 damage to each of them. Dont apply Weakness and Resistance for Benched Pokémon.
 Flip 1 coin. If heads, switch this Pokemon with 1 of your Benched Pokémon.
 Flip 1 coin. If heads, until the end of your opponents next turn the Defending Pokémon cant attack or retreat.
 Flip 1 coin. If heads, look at your opponents hand. If he or she has any Trainer cards there, choose 1 of them. Your opponent shuffles that card into his or her deck.
 Remove 2 damage counters from this Pokemon for each Energy attached to it. If it has fewer damage counters than that, remove all of them.
 Flip 1 coin. If heads, this attack does 30 damage plus 30 more damage.
 Search your deck for 1 basic Energy card and attach it to 1 of your Pokémon. Shuffle your deck afterward.
 If there are any damage counters on this Pokemon, remove 1 of them.
 If the Defending Pokémon already has any damage counters on it, this attack does 40 damage plus 20 more damage. If not, this attack does 40 damage.
 The Defending Pokémon cant retreat during your opponents next turn.
 Flip 1 coin. If heads, choose 1 Special Condition Asleep, Burned, Confused, Paralyzed, or Poisoned. The Defending Pokémon is now affected by that Special Condition.
 Flip 2 coins. For each heads, remove 1 damage counter from each of your Pokémon. If 1 Pokémon has fewer damage counters than the number of heads, remove all of them.
 If your opponent has any Benched Pokémon, choose 1 of them and switch it with the Defending Pokémon.
 Flip 3 coins. This attack does 20 damage plus 10 more damage for each heads.
 If the Pokémon using this attack has Fire and Lightning basic Energy cards attached to it, the Defending Pokémon is now Confused. If the Pokémon using this attack has Fire and Fighting basic Energy cards attached to it, this attack does 30 damage plus 10 more damage and remove 3 damage counters from the Pokémon that Miracle Plate α is attached to.
 If the Pokémon using this attack has Fire and Water basic Energy cards attached to it, this attack does 30 damage plus 10 more damage and the Defending Pokémon is now Burned. If the Pokémon using this attack has Water and Psychic basic Energy cards attached to it, choose an Energy card attached to the Defending Pokémon, if any, and your opponent shuffles that card into his or her deck.
 If the Pokémon using this attack has Grass and Lightning basic Energy cards attached to it, the Defending Pokémon is now Asleep and Poisoned. If the Pokémon using this attack has Water and Lightning basic Energy cards attached to it, this attack does 30 damage plus 10 more damage and lets you put 1 damage counter on each of your opponents Benched Pokémon.
 If your opponent has 5 or more Prizes, search your deck for 1 Trainer card, show it to your opponent, and put it into your hand. If your opponent has only 1 Prize, the Defending Pokémon is now Burned, Paralyzed, and Poisoned.
 If your opponent has 5 or more Prizes, draw 3 cards. If your opponent has only 1 Prize, choose 2 Energy cards attached to the Defending Pokémon 1 if there is only 1. Your opponent shuffles those cards into his or her deck.
 If your opponent has 5 or more Prizes, shuffle your hand into your deck and then draw 6 cards. If your opponent has exactly 2 Prizes, choose 1 of your opponents Evolved Pokémon. Your opponent puts the top card on that Evolved Pokémon on the bottom of his or her deck. This counts as devolving that Pokémon.
 If your opponent has 5 or more Prizes, search your deck for up to 3 basic Energy cards, show them to your opponent, and put them into your hand. Shuffle your deck afterward. If your opponent has exactly 2 Prizes, remove all damage counters from 1 of your Pokémon.
 Remove 2 damage counters from this Pokemon and each Pokémon thats the same type color as this Pokemon.
 Discard an Energy card attached to this Pokemon.
 Discard an Energy card attached to this Pokemon and flip 1 coin. If heads, the Defending Pokémon is now Burned.
 Remove 1 damage counter from this Pokemon.
